which establishes the RoleType enum with four values: RoleNone, RoleViewer, RoleEditor, and RoleAdmin. A precedence map (rolePrecedence) assigns numeric levels to each role (10, 20, 30, 40 respectively), and the Includes() method determines role hierarchy—Admin includes Editor and Viewer, Editor includes Viewer. The roles are mirrored in `pkg/services/org/model.go` for backward compatibility.\\n\\n## Role-to-Permission Mapping\\nThe basic role definitions are created in `pkg/services/accesscontrol/roles.go` via the BuildBasicRoleDefinitions() function, which returns a map of RoleType strings to RoleDTO objects. role-based permission model (Viewer/Editor/Admin) through several coordinated components:\\n\\n## Role Definition\\nThe core three-tier model is defined in `pkg/apimachinery/identity/role_type.go`, which establishes the RoleType enum with four values: RoleNone, RoleViewer, RoleEditor, and RoleAdmin. A precedence map (rolePrecedence) assigns numeric levels to each role (10, 20, 30, 40 respectively), and the Includes() method determines role hierarchy—Admin includes Editor and Viewer, Editor includes Viewer. The roles are mirrored in `pkg/services/org/model.go` for backward compatibility.\\n\\n## Role-to-Permission Mapping\\nThe basic role definitions are created in `pkg/services/accesscontrol/roles.go` via the BuildBasicRoleDefinitions() function, which returns a map of RoleType strings to RoleDTO objects. These basic roles are initialized with empty permission arrays.\\n\\nThe actual permission assignments for Viewer/Editor/Admin roles are performed in:\\n- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/ossaccesscontrol/dashboard.go`: registerDashboardRoles() maps Viewer → read, Editor → read+write+delete, Admin → read+write+delete+permissions\\n- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/ossaccesscontrol/folder.go`: registerFolderRoles() applies similar permissions for folders, plus additional folder-specific actions\\n\\nThese permissions are granted to built-in roles through RoleRegistration objects with Grants fields that map to organization role strings.\\n\\n## Permission Guard Middleware\\nThe permission enforcement occurs through the middleware chain:\\n\\n1. **Request Authentication**: `pkg/middleware/auth.go` provides basic authentication middleware that validates user credentials\\n\\n2. **Access Control Middleware**: `pkg/services/accesscontrol/middleware.go` contains the Middleware() function which wraps an Evaluator. The middleware calls authorize() which evaluates whether the user has required permissions\\n\\n3. **Permission Evaluation**: `pkg/services/accesscontrol/acimpl/service.go` implements GetUserPermissions() and getUserPermissions(), which retrieve permissions by looking up the user's org roles (via GetOrgRoles in `pkg/services/accesscontrol/accesscontrol.go`) and retrieving the mapped permissions from the basic role definitions\\n\\n4. **Role Checking**: `pkg/apimachinery/identity/static.go` implements HasRole() on the Requester interface, which checks if the user's OrgRole.Includes() the requested role. Grafana Admins always return true\\n\\n## Dashboard/Folder Inheritance\\nDashboard and folder permissions are managed through:\\n\\n1. **Dashboard Permissions API**: `pkg/api/dashboard_permission.go` provides endpoints to get and update dashboard permissions using the dashboardPermissionMap that translates \\\"View\\\", \\\"Edit\\\", \\\"Admin\\\" to PERMISSION_VIEW, PERMISSION_EDIT, PERMISSION_ADMIN values\\n\\n2. **Folder Permissions API**: `pkg/api/folder_permission.go` provides similar endpoints for folder permissions\\n\\n3. **Permission Levels**: `pkg/services/dashboards/dashboardaccess/dashboard_access.go` defines the three permission types as bitwise flags: PERMISSION_VIEW (1), PERMISSION_EDIT (2), PERMISSION_ADMIN (4)\\n\\n4. **Permission Inheritance**: `pkg/services/accesscontrol/ossaccesscontrol/dashboard.go` includes an InheritedScopesSolver that determines inherited permissions by looking up dashboard.FolderUID and calling GetInheritedScopes(). Similarly, `pkg/services/accesscontrol/ossaccesscontrol/folder.go` has an InheritedScopesSolver for folder parent permissions\\n\\n5. **Folder Hierarchy Reconciliation**: `apps/iam/pkg/reconcilers/folder_reconciler.go` implements the FolderReconciler which reconciles folder parent relationships and updates permission inheritance when folders are created, updated, or deleted\\n\\n## Client-Side Permission Display\\nThe frontend receives permission information through:\\n- `apps/dashboard/pkg/apis/dashboard/types.go`: DashboardAccess struct with boolean flags (CanSave, CanEdit, CanAdmin)\\n- `pkg/api/dashboard.go`: Sets these flags by evaluating user permissions using AccessControl.Evaluate()\\n- `pkg/api/dtos/acl.go`: UpdateDashboardACLCommand structures for permission management\\n\\nThe complete flow: user role → GetOrgRoles → permission lookup from basic role definitions → middleware authorization checks → access allowed/denied with appropriate permission level (View/Edit/Admin).\"\n   254→}\n   255→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. A precedence map (rolePrecedence) assigns numeric levels to each role (10, 20, 30, 40 respectively), and the Includes() method determines role hierarchy—Admin includes Editor and Viewer, Editor includes Viewer. The roles are mirrored in `pkg/services/org/model.go` for backward compatibility.\\n\\n## Role-to-Permission Mapping\\nThe basic role definitions are created in `pkg/services/accesscontrol/roles.go` via the BuildBasicRoleDefinitions() function, which returns a map of RoleType strings to RoleDTO objects. These basic roles are initialized with empty permission arrays.\\n\\nThe actual permission assignments for Viewer/Editor/Admin roles are performed in:\\n- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/ossaccesscontrol/dashboard.go`: registerDashboardRoles() maps Viewer → read, Editor → read+write+delete, Admin → read+write+delete+permissions\\n- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/ossaccesscontrol/folder.go`: registerFolderRoles() applies similar permissions for folders, plus additional folder-specific actions\\n\\nThese permissions are granted to built-in roles through RoleRegistration objects with Grants fields that map to organization role strings.\\n\\n## Permission Guard Middleware\\nThe permission enforcement occurs through the middleware chain:\\n\\n1. **Request Authentication**: `pkg/middleware/auth.go` provides basic authentication middleware that validates user credentials\\n\\n2. **Access Control Middleware**: `pkg/services/accesscontrol/middleware.go` contains the Middleware() function which wraps an Evaluator. The middleware calls authorize() which evaluates whether the user has required permissions\\n\\n3. **Permission Evaluation**: `pkg/services/accesscontrol/acimpl/service.go` implements GetUserPermissions() and getUserPermissions(), which retrieve permissions by looking up the user's org roles (via GetOrgRoles in `pkg/services/accesscontrol/accesscontrol.go`) and retrieving the mapped permissions from the basic role definitions\\n\\n4. **Role Checking**: `pkg/apimachinery/identity/static.go` implements HasRole() on the Requester interface, which checks if the user's OrgRole.Includes() the requested role. Grafana Admins always return true\\n\\n## Dashboard/Folder Inheritance\\nDashboard and folder permissions are managed through:\\n\\n1. **Dashboard Permissions API**: `pkg/api/dashboard_permission.go` provides endpoints to get and update dashboard permissions using the dashboardPermissionMap that translates \\\"View\\\", \\\"Edit\\\", \\\"Admin\\\" to PERMISSION_VIEW, PERMISSION_EDIT, PERMISSION_ADMIN values\\n\\n2. **Folder Permissions API**: `pkg/api/folder_permission.go` provides similar endpoints for folder permissions\\n\\n3. **Permission Levels**: `pkg/services/dashboards/dashboardaccess/dashboard_access.go` defines the three permission types as bitwise flags: PERMISSION_VIEW (1), PERMISSION_EDIT (2), PERMISSION_ADMIN (4)\\n\\n4. **Permission Inheritance**: `pkg/services/accesscontrol/ossaccesscontrol/dashboard.go` includes an InheritedScopesSolver that determines inherited permissions by looking up dashboard.FolderUID and calling GetInheritedScopes(). Similarly, `pkg/services/accesscontrol/ossaccesscontrol/folder.go` has an InheritedScopesSolver for folder parent permissions\\n\\n5. **Folder Hierarchy Reconciliation**: `apps/iam/pkg/reconcilers/folder_reconciler.go` implements the FolderReconciler which reconciles folder parent relationships and updates permission inheritance when folders are created, updated, or deleted\\n\\n## Client-Side Permission Display\\nThe frontend receives permission information through:\\n- `apps/dashboard/pkg/apis/dashboard/types.go`: DashboardAccess struct with boolean flags (CanSave, CanEdit, CanAdmin)\\n- `pkg/api/dashboard.go`: Sets these flags by evaluating user permissions using AccessControl.Evaluate()\\n- `pkg/api/dtos/acl.go`: UpdateDashboardACLCommand structures for permission management\\n\\nThe complete flow: user role → GetOrgRoles → permission lookup from basic role definitions → middleware authorization checks → access allowed/denied with appropriate permission level (View/Edit/Admin).\"\n}\n","numLines":255,"startLine":1,"totalLines":255}}}
